既存ノートとの関係を一言で言うと
================

あなたの今のノートは、主に

**「戦略を作るノート」**

です。  
ここに今回の差し込みを入れると、

**「戦略を作って、その仮説と収益源泉まで検証するノート」**

になります。

つまり、差し込み位置の基本原則は

*   **生成されたものは、その直後で検証する**
*   **大きな識別分析は最後にまとめる**

です。

* * *

実際の並べ方の簡易版
==========

本当に簡単に言うと、セルをこの順で並べてください。

1.  rolling PCA の直後  
    → diagnostics, PCA factor attribution
2.  weights\_factor の直後  
    → AR(1), timed vs untimed, TSFM vs CSFM, continuous TSFM
3.  weights\_etf / weights\_etf\_reg の直後  
    → mapping validation, condbeta mapping
4.  final backtest の直後  
    → FF attribution, rolling beta, decomposition, residualized strategy, benchmark, robustness

* * *

必要なら次に、  
**あなたが今持っている既存セル名に合わせて「このセルの後ろにこのコード」と1対1で対応づけた挿入表**を作ります。

## Prompt:
フルコードで示して

## Response:
思考時間: 5s

以下は、**既存ノートの後半を置き換える／追記するためのフルコード**です。  
内容は次を一通り含みます。

*   rolling PCA による latent factor 抽出
*   factor diagnostics
*   factor momentum 検証
*   continuous TSFM
*   loading-based / regression-based / conditional-beta mapping
*   Fama-French 5因子 + Mom の読込
*   伝統因子 attribution
*   FF 残差化後の再PCA・再戦略
*   benchmark / robustness
*   図表出力

この構成は、  
**テーマ投資を伝統因子と追加的テーマ成分に分けて扱う視点**、  
**因子モメンタムの timing 効果**、  
**条件付きベータの解釈**  
をそれぞれ検証できるようにしたものです。

* * *

```
# ============================================================
# FULL NOTEBOOK CODE
# Thematic ETF Latent Factor Timing + Traditional Factor Analysis
# ============================================================

import os
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import statsmodels.api as sm

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 0. CONFIG
# ------------------------------------------------------------
CONFIG = {
    # data frequency
    "periods_per_year": 252,   # daily base
    "rebalance_freq": "W-FRI", # or "M"

    # rolling PCA
    "pca_window": 126,         # ~6 months trading days
    "pca_min_periods": 63,
    "n_factors": 3,

    # factor momentum
    # (start_lag, end_lag, weight)
    "mom_specs": [
        (1, 1, 1.0),
        (2, 12, 1.0),
        (13, 60, 0.5),
    ],
    "signal_vol_window": 63,
    "signal_vol_min_periods": 21,
    "signal_clip": 3.0,

    # rolling regressions
    "beta_window": 126,
    "beta_min_periods": 63,

    # FF residualization
    "ff_resid_window": 126,
    "ff_resid_min_periods": 63,

    # transaction cost
    "cost_one_way": 0.0005,  # 5 bps one-way example

    # output
    "save_outputs": False,
    "output_dir": "./outputs",
}

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 1. IO / HELPERS
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def ensure_datetime_index(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
    out = df.copy()
    out.index = pd.to_datetime(out.index)
    return out.sort_index()

def annualize_return(r, periods_per_year=252):
    r = pd.Series(r).dropna()
    if len(r) == 0:
        return np.nan
    return (1 + r).prod() ** (periods_per_year / len(r)) - 1

def annualize_vol(r, periods_per_year=252):
    r = pd.Series(r).dropna()
    if len(r) == 0:
        return np.nan
    return r.std(ddof=1) * np.sqrt(periods_per_year)

def sharpe_ratio(r, periods_per_year=252):
    r = pd.Series(r).dropna()
    vol = annualize_vol(r, periods_per_year)
    if pd.isna(vol) or vol == 0:
        return np.nan
    return annualize_return(r, periods_per_year) / vol

def max_drawdown(r):
    r = pd.Series(r).fillna(0.0)
    nav = (1 + r).cumprod()
    dd = nav / nav.cummax() - 1
    return dd.min()

def perf_stats(r, periods_per_year=252):
    return {
        "CAGR": annualize_return(r, periods_per_year),
        "AnnVol": annualize_vol(r, periods_per_year),
        "Sharpe": sharpe_ratio(r, periods_per_year),
        "MaxDD": max_drawdown(r),
        "N": pd.Series(r).dropna().shape[0],
    }

def perf_table(returns_dict, periods_per_year=252):
    rows = []
    for name, r in returns_dict.items():
        if r is None:
            continue
        s = perf_stats(r, periods_per_year)
        s["strategy"] = name
        rows.append(s)
    if len(rows) == 0:
        return pd.DataFrame()
    return pd.DataFrame(rows).set_index("strategy").sort_values("Sharpe", ascending=False)

def ols_with_hac(y, X, nw_lags=5):
    y = pd.Series(y).rename("y")
    X = pd.DataFrame(X).copy()
    df = pd.concat([y, X], axis=1).dropna()
    Y = df["y"]
    XX = sm.add_constant(df.drop(columns="y"), has_constant="add")
    return sm.OLS(Y, XX).fit(cov_type="HAC", cov_kwds={"maxlags": nw_lags})

def rolling_factor_regression(y, X, window=126, min_periods=63):
    y = pd.Series(y).rename("y")
    X = pd.DataFrame(X).copy()
    idx = y.index.intersection(X.index)
    y = y.reindex(idx)
    X = X.reindex(idx)

    out = pd.DataFrame(index=idx, columns=["alpha"] + list(X.columns), dtype=float)

    for i, dt in enumerate(idx):
        start = max(0, i - window + 1)
        win_idx = idx[start:i+1]
        df = pd.concat([y.loc[win_idx], X.loc[win_idx]], axis=1).dropna()
        if len(df) < min_periods:
            continue
        Y = df["y"]
        XX = sm.add_constant(df.drop(columns="y"), has_constant="add")
        res = sm.OLS(Y, XX).fit()
        out.loc[dt] = res.params.reindex(out.columns)
    return out

def normalize_long_only_row(x):
    x = pd.Series(x).clip(lower=0).fillna(0.0)
    denom = x.sum()
    if denom == 0:
        return x * 0.0
    return x / denom

def normalize_long_short_row(x):
    x = pd.Series(x).fillna(0.0)
    denom = x.abs().sum()
    if denom == 0:
        return x * 0.0
    return x / denom

def compute_turnover(weights: pd.DataFrame):
    return weights.fillna(0.0).diff().abs().sum(axis=1)

def concentration_hhi(weights: pd.DataFrame):
    return (weights.fillna(0.0) ** 2).sum(axis=1)

def save_table_csv(df, path):
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    df.to_csv(path, encoding="utf-8-sig")

def save_figure(fig, path):
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    fig.savefig(path, bbox_inches="tight", dpi=180)

def make_output_path(name, kind="tables"):
    return os.path.join(CONFIG["output_dir"], kind, name)

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 2. FAMA-FRENCH CSV LOADER
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def _find_ff_data_start(path, expected_header_tokens):
    with open(path, "r", errors="ignore") as f:
        lines = f.readlines()
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        line_clean = line.strip().replace(" ", "")
        if all(tok in line_clean for tok in expected_header_tokens):
            return i
    raise ValueError(f"Header not found in {path}")

def load_ff5_daily_csv(path):
    header_row = _find_ff_data_start(
        path,
        expected_header_tokens=["Mkt-RF", "SMB", "HML", "RMW", "CMA", "RF"]
    )
    df = pd.read_csv(path, skiprows=header_row)
    first_col = df.columns[0]
    df = df.rename(columns={first_col: "date"})
    df["date"] = pd.to_datetime(df["date"].astype(str), format="%Y%m%d", errors="coerce")
    df = df[df["date"].notna()].copy()

    cols = ["Mkt-RF", "SMB", "HML", "RMW", "CMA", "RF"]
    for c in cols:
        df[c] = pd.to_numeric(df[c], errors="coerce")

    df = df.replace([-99.99, -999.0, -999, -99.0], np.nan)
    df[cols] = df[cols] / 100.0
    df = df.set_index("date").sort_index()
    return df[cols]

def load_ff_mom_daily_csv(path):
    header_row = _find_ff_data_start(path, expected_header_tokens=["Mom"])
    df = pd.read_csv(path, skiprows=header_row)
    first_col = df.columns[0]
    df = df.rename(columns={first_col: "date"})
    df["date"] = pd.to_datetime(df["date"].astype(str), format="%Y%m%d", errors="coerce")
    df = df[df["date"].notna()].copy()

    mom_col = [c for c in df.columns if c.strip().lower() == "mom"]
    if len(mom_col) != 1:
        raise ValueError("Momentum column not found uniquely.")
    mom_col = mom_col[0]

    df[mom_col] = pd.to_numeric(df[mom_col], errors="coerce")
    df = df.replace([-99.99, -999.0, -999, -99.0], np.nan)
    df[mom_col] = df[mom_col] / 100.0
    df = df.rename(columns={mom_col: "Mom"})
    df = df.set_index("date").sort_index()
    return df[["Mom"]]

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 3. INPUTS
# ------------------------------------------------------------
# Required:
#   rets: ETF raw return DataFrame
# Optional:
#   volume_df: ETF volume DataFrame
#
# Example assumptions:
# rets = ...
# volume_df = ...

rets = ensure_datetime_index(rets)
if "volume_df" in globals():
    volume_df = ensure_datetime_index(volume_df).reindex(rets.index)[rets.columns]
else:
    volume_df = None

# FF files
ff5_path = "/mnt/data/F-F_Research_Data_5_Factors_2x3_daily.csv"
mom_path = "/mnt/data/F-F_Momentum_Factor_daily.csv"

ff5_daily = load_ff5_daily_csv(ff5_path)
mom_daily = load_ff_mom_daily_csv(mom_path)
trad_factor_rets = ff5_daily.join(mom_daily, how="inner").sort_index()

# Align
common_dates = rets.index.intersection(trad_factor_rets.index)
rets = rets.reindex(common_dates)
ff_aligned = trad_factor_rets.reindex(common_dates)

# ETF excess returns
rets_excess = rets.sub(ff_aligned["RF"], axis=0)

print("rets:", rets.shape, rets.index.min(), rets.index.max())
print("rets_excess:", rets_excess.shape)
print("ff_aligned:", ff_aligned.shape)

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 4. REBALANCE DATES
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def get_rebalance_dates(index, rule="W-FRI"):
    idx = pd.DatetimeIndex(index).sort_values().unique()
    if rule == "M":
        return idx.to_series().groupby(idx.to_period("M")).max().values
    if rule.startswith("W-"):
        return idx.to_series().groupby(idx.to_period(rule)).max().values
    raise ValueError("Unsupported rebalance rule")

rebalance_dates = pd.DatetimeIndex(get_rebalance_dates(rets.index, CONFIG["rebalance_freq"]))
rebalance_dates = rebalance_dates.intersection(rets.index)

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 5. ROLLING PCA
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def rolling_pca_from_returns(rets_input, n_factors=3, window=126, min_periods=63, rebalance_dates=None):
    rets_input = ensure_datetime_index(rets_input)
    if rebalance_dates is None:
        rebalance_dates = rets_input.index

    factor_cols = [f"PC{i+1}" for i in range(n_factors)]
    factor_ret_out = pd.DataFrame(index=rets_input.index, columns=factor_cols, dtype=float)
    explained_var_ratio_by_t = pd.DataFrame(index=rets_input.index, columns=factor_cols, dtype=float)
    loadings_out = {}

    dates = rets_input.index

    for dt in rebalance_dates:
        if dt not in dates:
            continue
        i = dates.get_loc(dt)
        start = max(0, i - window + 1)
        win = rets_input.iloc[start:i+1].copy()
        win = win.dropna(axis=0, how="any")
        if len(win) < min_periods:
            continue
        if win.shape[1] < n_factors:
            continue

        X = win.values
        X = X - X.mean(axis=0, keepdims=True)
        cov = np.cov(X, rowvar=False)

        eigvals, eigvecs = np.linalg.eigh(cov)
        idx = np.argsort(eigvals)[::-1]
        eigvals = eigvals[idx]
        eigvecs = eigvecs[:, idx]

        P = eigvecs[:, :n_factors]
        evr = eigvals[:n_factors] / np.maximum(eigvals.sum(), 1e-12)

        r_now = rets_input.loc[dt]
        if r_now.isna().any():
            continue

        f_now = P.T @ r_now.values
        factor_ret_out.loc[dt, factor_cols] = f_now
        explained_var_ratio_by_t.loc[dt, factor_cols] = evr
        loadings_out[dt] = P

    # forward-fill factor loadings over non-rebalance dates if needed
    # factor returns only at rebalance dates by construction; for diagnostics/backtests we align later
    return factor_ret_out, loadings_out, explained_var_ratio_by_t

factor_ret_raw, loadings_by_t, explained_var_ratio_by_t = rolling_pca_from_returns(
    rets_input=rets_excess,
    n_factors=CONFIG["n_factors"],
    window=CONFIG["pca_window"],
    min_periods=CONFIG["pca_min_periods"],
    rebalance_dates=rebalance_dates,
)

factor_ret = factor_ret_raw.copy()

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 6. FACTOR DIAGNOSTICS
# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 6.1 EVR
cum_evr = explained_var_ratio_by_t.cumsum(axis=1)

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 5))
cum_evr.dropna(how="all").plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.8)
ax.set_title("Cumulative Explained Variance Ratio Over Time")
ax.set_ylabel("Cum EVR")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

table_evr = pd.DataFrame({
    "mean_evr": explained_var_ratio_by_t.mean(),
    "median_evr": explained_var_ratio_by_t.median(),
    "mean_cum_evr": cum_evr.mean(),
})
display(table_evr)

# 6.2 Reconstruction error
def reconstruction_error(rets_input, factor_ret_df, loadings_dict, valid_cols):
    errs = []
    common = rets_input.index.intersection(factor_ret_df.dropna(how="all").index)
    for dt in common:
        if dt not in loadings_dict:
            continue
        B = loadings_dict[dt]
        r = rets_input.loc[dt, valid_cols].values.reshape(-1, 1)
        f = factor_ret_df.loc[dt].values.reshape(-1, 1)
        if np.isnan(r).any() or np.isnan(f).any():
            continue
        r_hat = B @ f
        mse = np.mean((r.flatten() - r_hat.flatten()) ** 2)
        errs.append((dt, mse))
    return pd.Series(dict(errs)).sort_index()

valid_cols = rets_excess.columns.tolist()
recon_mse = reconstruction_error(rets_excess, factor_ret, loadings_by_t, valid_cols)

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 4))
recon_mse.plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.5)
ax.set_title("Reconstruction MSE Over Time")
ax.set_ylabel("MSE")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

# 6.3 Loading stability
def loading_stability(loadings_dict):
    dates = sorted(loadings_dict.keys())
    rows = []
    for t0, t1 in zip(dates[:-1], dates[1:]):
        B0 = loadings_dict[t0]
        B1 = loadings_dict[t1]
        k = min(B0.shape[1], B1.shape[1])
        for j in range(k):
            x = B0[:, j]
            y = B1[:, j]
            corr = np.corrcoef(x, y)[0, 1]
            if pd.notna(corr) and corr < 0:
                y = -y
                corr = np.corrcoef(x, y)[0, 1]
            rows.append({"date": t1, "factor": f"PC{j+1}", "corr": corr})
    return pd.DataFrame(rows)

stab_df = loading_stability(loadings_by_t)
stab_pivot = stab_df.pivot(index="date", columns="factor", values="corr")

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 4))
stab_pivot.plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.5)
ax.set_title("Consecutive Loading Correlation")
ax.set_ylabel("corr(B_t, B_{t-1})")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

# 6.4 Top exposure ETFs
def top_exposure_etfs(loadings_dict, etf_cols, top_n=3):
    rows = []
    for dt, B in loadings_dict.items():
        cols = [f"PC{i+1}" for i in range(B.shape[1])]
        df = pd.DataFrame(B, index=etf_cols, columns=cols)
        for c in df.columns:
            s = df[c].abs().sort_values(ascending=False).head(top_n)
            rows.append({
                "date": dt,
                "factor": c,
                "top_etfs": ", ".join(s.index.tolist())
            })
    return pd.DataFrame(rows)

top_exp = top_exposure_etfs(loadings_by_t, rets_excess.columns, top_n=3)
display(top_exp.tail(12))

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 7. FACTOR MOMENTUM
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def make_composite_factor_mom(factor_ret_df, specs):
    out = pd.DataFrame(0.0, index=factor_ret_df.index, columns=factor_ret_df.columns)
    for start_lag, end_lag, w in specs:
        part = pd.DataFrame(index=factor_ret_df.index, columns=factor_ret_df.columns, dtype=float)
        for c in factor_ret_df.columns:
            vals = []
            s = factor_ret_df[c]
            for i in range(len(s)):
                left = i - end_lag
                right = i - start_lag + 1
                if left < 0 or right <= left:
                    vals.append(np.nan)
                else:
                    vals.append(s.iloc[left:right].sum())
            part[c] = vals
        out = out.add(w * part, fill_value=0.0)
    return out

def rolling_factor_vol(factor_ret_df, window=63, min_periods=21):
    return factor_ret_df.rolling(window, min_periods=min_periods).std()

factor_mom = make_composite_factor_mom(factor_ret, CONFIG["mom_specs"])
factor_vol = rolling_factor_vol(
    factor_ret,
    window=CONFIG["signal_vol_window"],
    min_periods=CONFIG["signal_vol_min_periods"]
)

signal_scaled = factor_mom / factor_vol.replace(0, np.nan)
signal_scaled = signal_scaled.clip(-CONFIG["signal_clip"], CONFIG["signal_clip"])

# 7.1 Base discrete weights (top-1)
weights_factor = pd.DataFrame(0.0, index=signal_scaled.index, columns=signal_scaled.columns)
for dt in signal_scaled.index:
    s = signal_scaled.loc[dt].dropna()
    if len(s) == 0:
        continue
    top = s.sort_values(ascending=False).index[:1]
    weights_factor.loc[dt, top] = 1.0

# 7.2 Continuous TSFM weights
weights_factor_cont = pd.DataFrame(index=signal_scaled.index, columns=signal_scaled.columns, dtype=float)
for dt in signal_scaled.index:
    weights_factor_cont.loc[dt] = normalize_long_only_row(signal_scaled.loc[dt])
weights_factor_cont = weights_factor_cont.fillna(0.0)

# 7.3 AR(1)
def ar1_table(factor_ret_df, nw_lags=5):
    rows = []
    for c in factor_ret_df.columns:
        df = pd.concat([
            factor_ret_df[c].shift(-1).rename("y"),
            factor_ret_df[c].rename("x")
        ], axis=1).dropna()
        if len(df) < 24:
            continue
        X = sm.add_constant(df["x"])
        res = sm.OLS(df["y"], X).fit(cov_type="HAC", cov_kwds={"maxlags": nw_lags})
        rows.append({
            "factor": c,
            "phi": res.params["x"],
            "t_phi": res.tvalues["x"],
            "p_phi": res.pvalues["x"],
            "n_obs": len(df),
        })
    return pd.DataFrame(rows).set_index("factor").sort_values("phi", ascending=False)

table_ar1 = ar1_table(factor_ret)
display(table_ar1)

# 7.4 formation efficacy
def compute_factor_mom_window(factor_ret_df, start_lag, end_lag):
    out = pd.DataFrame(index=factor_ret_df.index, columns=factor_ret_df.columns, dtype=float)
    for c in factor_ret_df.columns:
        vals = []
        s = factor_ret_df[c]
        for i in range(len(s)):
            left = i - end_lag
            right = i - start_lag + 1
            if left < 0 or right <= left:
                vals.append(np.nan)
            else:
                vals.append(s.iloc[left:right].sum())
        out[c] = vals
    return out

mom_1_1 = compute_factor_mom_window(factor_ret, 1, 1)
mom_2_12 = compute_factor_mom_window(factor_ret, 2, 12)
mom_13_60 = compute_factor_mom_window(factor_ret, 13, 60)

def pooled_predictability(signal_df, future_ret_df, nw_lags=5):
    rows = []
    common_cols = signal_df.columns.intersection(future_ret_df.columns)
    for c in common_cols:
        df = pd.concat([
            future_ret_df[c].shift(-1).rename("y"),
            signal_df[c].rename("x")
        ], axis=1).dropna()
        if len(df) == 0:
            continue
        df["factor"] = c
        rows.append(df)
    if len(rows) == 0:
        return None, None
    panel = pd.concat(rows, axis=0)
    X = sm.add_constant(panel["x"])
    res = sm.OLS(panel["y"], X).fit(cov_type="HAC", cov_kwds={"maxlags": nw_lags})
    return res, panel

rows = []
for name, sig in {"1_1": mom_1_1, "2_12": mom_2_12, "13_60": mom_13_60}.items():
    res, panel = pooled_predictability(sig, factor_ret)
    if res is not None:
        rows.append({
            "spec": name,
            "coef": res.params["x"],
            "t": res.tvalues["x"],
            "p": res.pvalues["x"],
            "n": len(panel),
        })
table_signal_predict = pd.DataFrame(rows).set_index("spec")
display(table_signal_predict)

# 7.5 factor returns
def portfolio_return_from_weights(weights, rets_input):
    return (weights.shift(1).reindex(rets_input.index).fillna(0.0) * rets_input).sum(axis=1)

raw_factor_ret = factor_ret.mean(axis=1).rename("raw_factor_eq")
timed_factor_ret = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_factor, factor_ret).rename("timed_factor")
timed_factor_ret_cont = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_factor_cont, factor_ret).rename("timed_factor_cont")

factor_compare = pd.concat([raw_factor_ret, timed_factor_ret, timed_factor_ret_cont], axis=1).dropna()

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 5))
((1 + factor_compare).cumprod()).plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.8)
ax.set_title("Timed vs Untimed Factor Portfolios")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

display(perf_table({
    "Raw factor EQ": raw_factor_ret,
    "Timed factor (discrete)": timed_factor_ret,
    "Timed factor (continuous)": timed_factor_ret_cont,
}, CONFIG["periods_per_year"]))

# 7.6 CSFM
def csfm_weights(signal_df, top_n=1, bottom_n=1):
    w = pd.DataFrame(0.0, index=signal_df.index, columns=signal_df.columns)
    for dt in signal_df.index:
        s = signal_df.loc[dt].dropna().sort_values()
        if len(s) < top_n + bottom_n:
            continue
        low = s.index[:bottom_n]
        high = s.index[-top_n:]
        w.loc[dt, high] = 1.0 / top_n
        w.loc[dt, low] = -1.0 / bottom_n
    return w

weights_csfm = csfm_weights(mom_2_12, top_n=1, bottom_n=1)
ret_csfm = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_csfm, factor_ret).rename("CSFM")
ret_tsfm = timed_factor_ret_cont.rename("TSFM")

table_tsfm_csfm = perf_table({"TSFM": ret_tsfm, "CSFM": ret_csfm}, CONFIG["periods_per_year"])
display(table_tsfm_csfm)

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 8. MAPPING
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def map_factor_to_etf_loading(weights_factor_like, loadings_dict, etf_cols, long_only=True):
    out = pd.DataFrame(0.0, index=weights_factor_like.index, columns=etf_cols)
    common_dates = sorted(set(weights_factor_like.index).intersection(loadings_dict.keys()))
    for dt in common_dates:
        wf = weights_factor_like.loc[dt].fillna(0.0).values.reshape(-1, 1)
        B = loadings_dict[dt]
        k = min(B.shape[1], len(wf))
        raw = pd.Series((B[:, :k] @ wf[:k]).ravel(), index=etf_cols)
        out.loc[dt] = normalize_long_only_row(raw) if long_only else normalize_long_short_row(raw)
    return out.fillna(0.0)

weights_etf = map_factor_to_etf_loading(weights_factor, loadings_by_t, rets.columns, long_only=True)
weights_etf_cont_loading = map_factor_to_etf_loading(weights_factor_cont, loadings_by_t, rets.columns, long_only=True)

ret_etf_loading = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_etf, rets).rename("etf_loading")
ret_etf_cont_loading = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_etf_cont_loading, rets).rename("etf_cont_loading")

# 8.1 regression-based mimic
def estimate_rolling_betas_to_factors(rets_input, factor_ret_df, window=126, min_periods=63):
    betas = {}
    common_dates = rets_input.index.intersection(factor_ret_df.dropna(how="all").index)

    for i, dt in enumerate(common_dates):
        start = max(0, i - window + 1)
        win_dates = common_dates[start:i+1]

        B = pd.DataFrame(index=rets_input.columns, columns=factor_ret_df.columns, dtype=float)
        F = factor_ret_df.loc[win_dates]

        for etf in rets_input.columns:
            y = rets_input.loc[win_dates, etf]
            df = pd.concat([y, F], axis=1).dropna()
            if len(df) < min_periods:
                continue
            Y = df.iloc[:, 0]
            X = sm.add_constant(df.iloc[:, 1:])
            res = sm.OLS(Y, X).fit()
            B.loc[etf] = res.params.drop("const").reindex(factor_ret_df.columns)
        betas[dt] = B
    return betas

rolling_betas = estimate_rolling_betas_to_factors(
    rets, factor_ret, CONFIG["beta_window"], CONFIG["beta_min_periods"]
)

def map_factor_to_etf_regression(weights_factor_like, rolling_betas_dict, etf_cols, factor_cols, long_only=True):
    out = pd.DataFrame(0.0, index=weights_factor_like.index, columns=etf_cols)
    common_dates = sorted(set(weights_factor_like.index).intersection(rolling_betas_dict.keys()))
    for dt in common_dates:
        wf = weights_factor_like.loc[dt].reindex(factor_cols).fillna(0.0).values.reshape(-1, 1)
        B = rolling_betas_dict[dt].reindex(etf_cols)[factor_cols].fillna(0.0)
        raw = pd.Series((B.values @ wf).ravel(), index=etf_cols)
        out.loc[dt] = normalize_long_only_row(raw) if long_only else normalize_long_short_row(raw)
    return out.fillna(0.0)

weights_etf_reg = map_factor_to_etf_regression(
    weights_factor_cont, rolling_betas, rets.columns, factor_ret.columns, long_only=True
)
ret_etf_reg = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_etf_reg, rets).rename("etf_reg")

# 8.2 conditional-beta mapping (IPCA-lite)
char_mom12 = rets.shift(2).rolling(11).sum()
char_rev1 = -rets.shift(1)
char_vol12 = rets.rolling(12, min_periods=6).std()

char_dict = {"mom12": char_mom12, "rev1": char_rev1, "vol12": char_vol12}
if volume_df is not None:
    char_dict["volchg3"] = np.log1p(volume_df).diff(3)

chars_std = {}
for name, df in char_dict.items():
    z = df.copy()
    for dt in z.index:
        row = z.loc[dt]
        mu = row.mean()
        sd = row.std(ddof=1)
        if pd.isna(sd) or sd == 0:
            z.loc[dt] = np.nan
        else:
            z.loc[dt] = (row - mu) / sd
    chars_std[name] = z

def predict_conditional_betas(rolling_betas_dict, chars_std_dict, factor_cols):
    pred_betas = {}
    common_dates = sorted(set(rolling_betas_dict.keys()))
    for dt in common_dates:
        beta_df = rolling_betas_dict[dt].copy()
        z_parts = []
        for name, zdf in chars_std_dict.items():
            if dt in zdf.index:
                z_parts.append(zdf.loc[dt].rename(name))
        if len(z_parts) == 0:
            continue

        Z = pd.concat(z_parts, axis=1)
        Z = Z.reindex(beta_df.index)

        beta_hat_df = pd.DataFrame(index=beta_df.index, columns=factor_cols, dtype=float)

        for fac in factor_cols:
            y = beta_df[fac]
            df = pd.concat([y.rename("y"), Z], axis=1).dropna()
            if len(df) < max(5, Z.shape[1] + 2):
                continue
            Y = df["y"]
            X = sm.add_constant(df.drop(columns="y"))
            res = sm.OLS(Y, X).fit()

            X_all = sm.add_constant(Z, has_constant="add")
            X_all = X_all.reindex(columns=X.columns, fill_value=0.0)
            beta_hat_df.loc[X_all.index, fac] = res.predict(X_all)

        pred_betas[dt] = beta_hat_df
    return pred_betas

pred_cond_betas = predict_conditional_betas(rolling_betas, chars_std, factor_ret.columns)

def map_factor_to_etf_condbeta(weights_factor_like, pred_cond_betas_dict, etf_cols, factor_cols, long_only=True):
    out = pd.DataFrame(0.0, index=weights_factor_like.index, columns=etf_cols)
    common_dates = sorted(set(weights_factor_like.index).intersection(pred_cond_betas_dict.keys()))
    for dt in common_dates:
        wf = weights_factor_like.loc[dt].reindex(factor_cols).fillna(0.0).values.reshape(-1, 1)
        beta_hat = pred_cond_betas_dict[dt].reindex(etf_cols)[factor_cols].fillna(0.0)
        raw = pd.Series((beta_hat.values @ wf).ravel(), index=etf_cols)
        out.loc[dt] = normalize_long_only_row(raw) if long_only else normalize_long_short_row(raw)
    return out.fillna(0.0)

weights_etf_condbeta = map_factor_to_etf_condbeta(
    weights_factor_cont, pred_cond_betas, rets.columns, factor_ret.columns, long_only=True
)
ret_etf_condbeta = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_etf_condbeta, rets).rename("etf_condbeta")

# 8.3 Mapping validation
mapped_compare = pd.concat([
    timed_factor_ret_cont.rename("factor_target"),
    ret_etf_cont_loading,
    ret_etf_reg,
    ret_etf_condbeta
], axis=1).dropna()

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 5))
((1 + mapped_compare).cumprod()).plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.8)
ax.set_title("Factor Target vs ETF-Mapped Portfolios")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

display(perf_table({
    "Factor target": timed_factor_ret_cont,
    "ETF mapped loading": ret_etf_cont_loading,
    "ETF mapped reg": ret_etf_reg,
    "ETF mapped condbeta": ret_etf_condbeta,
}, CONFIG["periods_per_year"]))

def exposure_error(weights_etf_like, weights_factor_like, loadings_dict, etf_cols, factor_cols):
    vals = []
    common_dates = sorted(set(weights_etf_like.index).intersection(weights_factor_like.index).intersection(loadings_dict.keys()))
    for dt in common_dates:
        B = loadings_dict[dt]
        wE = weights_etf_like.loc[dt].reindex(etf_cols).fillna(0.0).values.reshape(-1, 1)
        wF = weights_factor_like.loc[dt].reindex(factor_cols).fillna(0.0).values.reshape(-1, 1)
        k = min(B.shape[1], len(factor_cols))
        implied = B[:, :k].T @ wE
        err = np.linalg.norm(implied - wF[:k])
        vals.append((dt, err))
    return pd.Series(dict(vals)).sort_index()

exp_err_loading = exposure_error(weights_etf_cont_loading, weights_factor_cont, loadings_by_t, rets.columns, factor_ret.columns)
exp_err_loading.name = "loading"

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 4))
exp_err_loading.plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.5)
ax.set_title("Exposure Replication Error (Loading Mapping)")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

diag_df = pd.DataFrame({
    "turnover_loading": compute_turnover(weights_etf_cont_loading),
    "turnover_reg": compute_turnover(weights_etf_reg),
    "turnover_condbeta": compute_turnover(weights_etf_condbeta),
    "hhi_loading": concentration_hhi(weights_etf_cont_loading),
    "hhi_reg": concentration_hhi(weights_etf_reg),
    "hhi_condbeta": concentration_hhi(weights_etf_condbeta),
})
display(diag_df.describe())

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 9. BENCHMARKS
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def simple_etf_mom_weights(rets_input, lookback=12, skip=1, top_n=3):
    signal = rets_input.shift(skip + 1).rolling(lookback).sum()
    w = pd.DataFrame(0.0, index=rets_input.index, columns=rets_input.columns)
    for dt in signal.index:
        s = signal.loc[dt].dropna().sort_values(ascending=False)
        if len(s) < top_n:
            continue
        top = s.index[:top_n]
        w.loc[dt, top] = 1.0 / top_n
    return w, signal

weights_etf_mom, etf_mom_signal = simple_etf_mom_weights(rets, lookback=12, skip=1, top_n=min(3, rets.shape[1]))
ret_etf_mom = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_etf_mom, rets).rename("ETF_mom")
ret_eqw = rets.mean(axis=1).rename("EQW_ETF")

benchmark_table = perf_table({
    "ETF mapped loading": ret_etf_cont_loading,
    "ETF mapped condbeta": ret_etf_condbeta,
    "ETF momentum benchmark": ret_etf_mom,
    "EQW ETF benchmark": ret_eqw,
}, CONFIG["periods_per_year"])
display(benchmark_table)

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 10. STATIC FACTOR ATTRIBUTION (TABLE 1)
# ------------------------------------------------------------
factor_cols = ["Mkt-RF", "SMB", "HML", "RMW", "CMA", "Mom"]

strategy_dict = {
    "Base_loading": ret_etf_loading,
    "Cont_loading": ret_etf_cont_loading,
    "CondBeta": ret_etf_condbeta,
    "RegMapped": ret_etf_reg,
}

rows = []
for name, r in strategy_dict.items():
    res = ols_with_hac(r, ff_aligned[factor_cols], nw_lags=5)
    row = {"strategy": name, "alpha": res.params["const"], "alpha_t": res.tvalues["const"], "R2": res.rsquared}
    for c in factor_cols:
        row[c] = res.params.get(c, np.nan)
        row[f"{c}_t"] = res.tvalues.get(c, np.nan)
    rows.append(row)

table1_factor_attr = pd.DataFrame(rows).set_index("strategy")
display(table1_factor_attr)

# 11. ROLLING FACTOR BETAS (FIGURE 1)
# ------------------------------------------------------------
target_strategy = ret_etf_cont_loading
rolling_betas_fig1 = rolling_factor_regression(
    y=target_strategy,
    X=ff_aligned[factor_cols],
    window=CONFIG["beta_window"],
    min_periods=CONFIG["beta_min_periods"]
)

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 6))
rolling_betas_fig1[["Mkt-RF", "HML", "Mom"]].plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.6)
ax.set_title("Figure 1. Rolling Factor Betas of Strategy")
ax.set_ylabel("Beta")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 12. EXPLAINED / UNEXPLAINED DECOMPOSITION (FIGURE 2)
# ------------------------------------------------------------
res_decomp = ols_with_hac(target_strategy, ff_aligned[factor_cols], nw_lags=5)

df_decomp = pd.concat([
    pd.Series(target_strategy).rename("strategy"),
    ff_aligned[factor_cols]
], axis=1).dropna()

X_full = sm.add_constant(df_decomp[factor_cols], has_constant="add")
df_decomp["explained"] = res_decomp.predict(X_full)
df_decomp["unexplained"] = df_decomp["strategy"] - df_decomp["explained"]

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 6))
((1 + df_decomp[["strategy", "explained", "unexplained"]]).cumprod()).plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.8)
ax.set_title("Figure 2. Cumulative Return Decomposition")
ax.set_ylabel("NAV")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 13. FF RESIDUALIZATION
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def residualize_returns_against_ff(rets_excess_df, ff_df, factor_cols=None, window=126, min_periods=63):
    if factor_cols is None:
        factor_cols = ["Mkt-RF", "SMB", "HML", "RMW", "CMA", "Mom"]

    resid = pd.DataFrame(index=rets_excess_df.index, columns=rets_excess_df.columns, dtype=float)
    betas = {}

    dates = rets_excess_df.index.intersection(ff_df.index)

    for i, dt in enumerate(dates):
        start = max(0, i - window + 1)
        win_dates = dates[start:i+1]

        X_win = ff_df.loc[win_dates, factor_cols]
        X_now = ff_df.loc[[dt], factor_cols]
        beta_df = pd.DataFrame(index=rets_excess_df.columns, columns=factor_cols, dtype=float)

        for etf in rets_excess_df.columns:
            y_win = rets_excess_df.loc[win_dates, etf]
            df = pd.concat([y_win.rename("y"), X_win], axis=1).dropna()
            if len(df) < min_periods:
                continue

            Y = df["y"]
            X = sm.add_constant(df[factor_cols])
            res = sm.OLS(Y, X).fit()

            x_now = sm.add_constant(X_now, has_constant="add")
            x_now = x_now.reindex(columns=X.columns, fill_value=0.0)

            y_hat = float(res.predict(x_now).iloc[0])
            if pd.notna(rets_excess_df.loc[dt, etf]):
                resid.loc[dt, etf] = rets_excess_df.loc[dt, etf] - y_hat

            beta_df.loc[etf, factor_cols] = res.params.reindex(["const"] + factor_cols).drop("const").values

        betas[dt] = beta_df

    return resid, betas

rets_resid_ff, rolling_ff_betas = residualize_returns_against_ff(
    rets_excess_df=rets_excess,
    ff_df=ff_aligned,
    factor_cols=factor_cols,
    window=CONFIG["ff_resid_window"],
    min_periods=CONFIG["ff_resid_min_periods"]
)

# Remove columns with too many NaNs for PCA
resid_cols = rets_resid_ff.dropna(axis=1, how="any").columns.tolist()
rets_resid_ff_clean = rets_resid_ff[resid_cols].copy()

factor_ret_resid_ff, loadings_by_t_resid_ff, explained_var_ratio_resid_ff = rolling_pca_from_returns(
    rets_input=rets_resid_ff_clean,
    n_factors=min(CONFIG["n_factors"], rets_resid_ff_clean.shape[1]),
    window=CONFIG["pca_window"],
    min_periods=CONFIG["pca_min_periods"],
    rebalance_dates=rebalance_dates.intersection(rets_resid_ff_clean.index)
)

factor_mom_resid_ff = make_composite_factor_mom(factor_ret_resid_ff, CONFIG["mom_specs"])
factor_vol_resid_ff = rolling_factor_vol(
    factor_ret_resid_ff,
    window=CONFIG["signal_vol_window"],
    min_periods=CONFIG["signal_vol_min_periods"]
)
signal_scaled_resid_ff = (factor_mom_resid_ff / factor_vol_resid_ff.replace(0, np.nan)).clip(-CONFIG["signal_clip"], CONFIG["signal_clip"])

weights_factor_resid_ff = pd.DataFrame(index=signal_scaled_resid_ff.index, columns=signal_scaled_resid_ff.columns, dtype=float)
for dt in signal_scaled_resid_ff.index:
    weights_factor_resid_ff.loc[dt] = normalize_long_only_row(signal_scaled_resid_ff.loc[dt])
weights_factor_resid_ff = weights_factor_resid_ff.fillna(0.0)

weights_etf_resid_ff = map_factor_to_etf_loading(
    weights_factor_like=weights_factor_resid_ff,
    loadings_dict=loadings_by_t_resid_ff,
    etf_cols=resid_cols,
    long_only=True
)

ret_factor_resid_ff = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_factor_resid_ff, factor_ret_resid_ff).rename("factor_resid_ff")
ret_etf_resid_ff = portfolio_return_from_weights(weights_etf_resid_ff, rets[resid_cols]).rename("etf_resid_ff")

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 14. ORIGINAL VS RESIDUALIZED (TABLE 2 / FIGURE 3)
# ------------------------------------------------------------
table2_original_vs_resid = perf_table({
    "Original_loading": ret_etf_cont_loading,
    "CondBeta": ret_etf_condbeta,
    "ResidualFF": ret_etf_resid_ff,
}, CONFIG["periods_per_year"])
display(table2_original_vs_resid)

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 6))
plot_df = pd.concat([
    ret_etf_cont_loading.rename("Original_loading"),
    ret_etf_condbeta.rename("CondBeta"),
    ret_etf_resid_ff.rename("ResidualFF"),
], axis=1).dropna(how="all")

((1 + plot_df.fillna(0.0)).cumprod()).plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.8)
ax.set_title("Figure 3. Original vs Residualized Strategy")
ax.set_ylabel("NAV")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 15. PCA FACTOR ATTRIBUTION (TABLE 3 / FIGURE 4)
# ------------------------------------------------------------
rows = []
for c in factor_ret.columns:
    res = ols_with_hac(factor_ret[c], ff_aligned[factor_cols], nw_lags=5)
    row = {"factor": c, "alpha": res.params["const"], "alpha_t": res.tvalues["const"], "R2": res.rsquared}
    for f in factor_cols:
        row[f] = res.params.get(f, np.nan)
        row[f"{f}_t"] = res.tvalues.get(f, np.nan)
    rows.append(row)
table3_pca_factor_attr = pd.DataFrame(rows).set_index("factor")
display(table3_pca_factor_attr)

heatmap_df = table3_pca_factor_attr[factor_cols].copy()
fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(8, 4))
im = ax.imshow(heatmap_df.values, aspect="auto")
ax.set_xticks(range(len(heatmap_df.columns)))

ax.set_yticklabels(heatmap_df.index)

fig.colorbar(im, ax=ax, fraction=0.046, pad=0.04)

# ------------------------------------------------------------

for name, r in {

}.items():
    res = ols_with_hac(r, ff_aligned[factor_cols], nw_lags=5)

    rows.append(row)

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 17. ROLLING ALPHA / R^2 (FIGURE 5)
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def rolling_alpha_r2(y, X, window=126, min_periods=63):
    y = pd.Series(y).rename("y")
    X = pd.DataFrame(X).copy()
    idx = y.index.intersection(X.index)
    out = pd.DataFrame(index=idx, columns=["alpha", "R2"], dtype=float)

    for i, dt in enumerate(idx):
        start = max(0, i - window + 1)
        win_idx = idx[start:i+1]
        df = pd.concat([y.loc[win_idx], X.loc[win_idx]], axis=1).dropna()
        if len(df) < min_periods:
            continue
        Y = df["y"]
        XX = sm.add_constant(df.drop(columns="y"), has_constant="add")
        res = sm.OLS(Y, XX).fit()
        out.loc[dt, "alpha"] = res.params["const"]
        out.loc[dt, "R2"] = res.rsquared
    return out

rolling_attr = rolling_alpha_r2(target_strategy, ff_aligned[factor_cols], CONFIG["beta_window"], CONFIG["beta_min_periods"])

fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 1, figsize=(12, 7), sharex=True)
rolling_attr["alpha"].plot(ax=axes[0], linewidth=1.5)
axes[0].set_title("Figure 5a. Rolling Alpha")
rolling_attr["R2"].plot(ax=axes[1], linewidth=1.5)
axes[1].set_title("Figure 5b. Rolling $R^2$")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 18. FACTOR CONTRIBUTION (FIGURE 6)
# ------------------------------------------------------------
res_static = ols_with_hac(target_strategy, ff_aligned[factor_cols], nw_lags=5)
df_contrib = ff_aligned[factor_cols].copy()
for c in factor_cols:
    df_contrib[c] = df_contrib[c] * res_static.params[c]
df_contrib["alpha"] = res_static.params["const"]

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 6))
df_contrib[factor_cols + ["alpha"]].cumsum().plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.3)
ax.set_title("Figure 6. Cumulative Additive Contributions by Traditional Factors")
ax.set_ylabel("Cumulative contribution")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 19. ORIGINAL / EXPLAINED / RESIDUALIZED (FIGURE 7)
# ------------------------------------------------------------
plot_all = pd.concat([
    pd.Series(target_strategy).rename("Original"),
    df_decomp["explained"].rename("Explained_by_FF"),
    ret_etf_resid_ff.rename("Residualized_strategy"),
], axis=1).dropna(how="all")

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 6))
((1 + plot_all.fillna(0.0)).cumprod()).plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.8)
ax.set_title("Figure 7. Original, FF-Explained, and Residualized Strategy")
ax.set_ylabel("NAV")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 20. SUBPERIOD / COST SENSITIVITY
# ------------------------------------------------------------
def subperiod_perf(r, split_dates, periods_per_year=252):
    r = pd.Series(r).dropna()
    out = []
    boundaries = [r.index.min()] + [pd.Timestamp(x) for x in split_dates] + [r.index.max()]
    for start, end in zip(boundaries[:-1], boundaries[1:]):
        sub = r.loc[(r.index >= start) & (r.index <= end)]
        if len(sub) == 0:
            continue
        out.append({
            "start": start,
            "end": end,
            "CAGR": annualize_return(sub, periods_per_year),
            "AnnVol": annualize_vol(sub, periods_per_year),
            "Sharpe": sharpe_ratio(sub, periods_per_year),
            "MaxDD": max_drawdown(sub),
            "N": len(sub),
        })
    return pd.DataFrame(out)

table_subperiod = subperiod_perf(
    ret_etf_cont_loading,
    split_dates=["2018-12-31", "2021-12-31"],
    periods_per_year=CONFIG["periods_per_year"]
)
display(table_subperiod)

turnover_loading = compute_turnover(weights_etf_cont_loading).reindex(ret_etf_cont_loading.index).fillna(0.0)
cost_grid = [0.0, 0.0005, 0.0010, 0.0020, 0.0050]
rows = []
for kappa in cost_grid:
    ret_net = ret_etf_cont_loading - kappa * turnover_loading
    rows.append({
        "one_way_cost": kappa,
        "CAGR": annualize_return(ret_net, CONFIG["periods_per_year"]),
        "AnnVol": annualize_vol(ret_net, CONFIG["periods_per_year"]),
        "Sharpe": sharpe_ratio(ret_net, CONFIG["periods_per_year"]),
        "MaxDD": max_drawdown(ret_net),
    })
table_cost = pd.DataFrame(rows)
display(table_cost)

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 21. SUMMARY TABLE
# ------------------------------------------------------------
summary_main = perf_table({
    "Raw factor EQ": raw_factor_ret,
    "Timed factor (disc)": timed_factor_ret,
    "Timed factor (cont)": timed_factor_ret_cont,
    "ETF loading": ret_etf_cont_loading,
    "ETF reg": ret_etf_reg,
    "ETF condbeta": ret_etf_condbeta,
    "ETF momentum benchmark": ret_etf_mom,
    "EQW ETF benchmark": ret_eqw,
    "ResidualFF": ret_etf_resid_ff,
}, CONFIG["periods_per_year"])
display(summary_main)

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 22. OPTIONAL SAVE
# ------------------------------------------------------------
if CONFIG["save_outputs"]:
    save_table_csv(table1_factor_attr, make_output_path("table1_factor_attribution.csv"))
    save_table_csv(table2_original_vs_resid, make_output_path("table2_original_vs_residualized.csv"))
    save_table_csv(table3_pca_factor_attr, make_output_path("table3_pca_factor_attribution.csv"))
    save_table_csv(table4_residualization_effect, make_output_path("table4_residualization_effect.csv"))
    save_table_csv(table_ar1, make_output_path("table_ar1_factors.csv"))
    save_table_csv(table_signal_predict, make_output_path("table_signal_predictability.csv"))
    save_table_csv(summary_main, make_output_path("table_summary_main.csv"))
    save_table_csv(table_subperiod, make_output_path("table_subperiod.csv"))
    save_table_csv(table_cost, make_output_path("table_cost_sensitivity.csv"))

print("Done.")
```

* * *

使い方
---

このコードは、基本的には

1.  `rets` を用意する
2.  上のフルコードを後半に貼る
3.  順に実行する

で動きます。

`rets` は **日次リターン DataFrame** を想定しています。  
価格しかない場合は、先に

```
rets = prices.pct_change().dropna()
```

で作ってください。

* * *

このコードで出る主要図表
------------

*   **Table 1**: strategy の FF5+Mom attribution
*   **Figure 1**: rolling factor betas
*   **Figure 2**: explained / unexplained decomposition
*   **Table 2**: original vs residualized performance
*   **Figure 3**: original vs residualized NAV
*   **Table 3**: PCA factor の FF5+Mom attribution
*   **Figure 4**: PCA factor attribution heatmap
*   **Table 4**: residualization effect
*   **Figure 5**: rolling alpha / rolling  $R^2$ 
*   **Figure 6**: factor contribution decomposition
*   **Figure 7**: original / explained / residualized comparison

* * *

実装上の注意
------

1.  **`rets` に欠損が多いと PCA が落ちやすい**  
    上場時期の違う ETF が多い場合は、  
    列ごとにサンプルを切るか、投資可能期間だけに絞る調整が必要です。
2.  **residualized PCA は列欠損に弱い**  
    ここでは簡単のため `dropna(axis=1, how="any")` 寄りにしています。  
    ETF 数が減りすぎるなら、列欠損の扱いを緩める調整が必要です。
3.  **conditional-beta mapping は IPCA の近似**  
    厳密な IPCA ではなく、ETF 特性から rolling beta を cross-section で近似予測する `IPCA-lite` です。  
    それでも「条件付きベータ写像が改善するか」を見るには十分です。
    Understanding Momentum and Reve…
4.  **日次頻度で 13-60 をそのまま使うと短い**  
    今回の `mom_specs` は、あなたの既存ノートの発想を尊重した形です。  
    日次でより厳密にやるなら、営業日ベースで horizon を再定義してもよいです。

* * *

必要なら次に、これを**あなたの今のノートの変数名に完全に合わせた版**へ調整します。

## Prompt:
お願いします

## Response:
ノート側の変数名に寄せるため、既存セルで実際に使われている名前を拾って対応版に落とします。主要な入出力だけ既存名に合わせれば、貼り替えやすくなります。

思考時間: 20s

了解です。  
ノートを確認したうえで、**既存の変数名・関数名に合わせた版**に落とします。

このノートで実際に使われている主要変数は次です。

*   価格: `px_d`
*   期間リターン: `ret_p`
*   潜在因子: `factor_ret`
*   PCA loadings: `loadings_by_t`
*   PCA eligibility: `eligibility_mask_by_t`
*   runtime: `RUNTIME`
*   既存関数:
    *   `build_rolling_pca`
    *   `compute_factor_mom`
    *   `allocate_factor_weights`
    *   `map_loadings_to_etf`
    *   `estimate_regression_betas`
    *   `run_backtest`
    *   `calc_metrics`
    *   `plot_equity_dd`

したがって、以下は**そのノートの後半にそのまま追記しやすい完全版**です。  
特に、FF日次CSVは `ret_p` の頻度に合わせて**月次/週次へ変換**して使います。

* * *

追加セル 1: Fama-French 日次CSVの読込と `ret_p` 頻度への変換
============================================

```
import os
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
import statsmodels.api as sm
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

def _find_ff_data_start(path, expected_header_tokens):
    with open(path, "r", errors="ignore") as f:
        lines = f.readlines()
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        line_clean = line.strip().replace(" ", "")
        if all(tok in line_clean for tok in expected_header_tokens):
            return i
    raise ValueError(f"Header not found in {path}")

def load_ff5_daily_csv(path):
    header_row = _find_ff_data_start(
        path,
        expected_header_tokens=["Mkt-RF", "SMB", "HML", "RMW", "CMA", "RF"]
    )
    df = pd.read_csv(path, skiprows=header_row)
    first_col = df.columns[0]
    df = df.rename(columns={first_col: "date"})
    df["date"] = pd.to_datetime(df["date"].astype(str), format="%Y%m%d", errors="coerce")
    df = df[df["date"].notna()].copy()

    cols = ["Mkt-RF", "SMB", "HML", "RMW", "CMA", "RF"]
    for c in cols:
        df[c] = pd.to_numeric(df[c], errors="coerce")

    df = df.replace([-99.99, -999.0, -999, -99.0], np.nan)
    df[cols] = df[cols] / 100.0
    df = df.set_index("date").sort_index()
    return df[cols]

def load_ff_mom_daily_csv(path):
    header_row = _find_ff_data_start(path, expected_header_tokens=["Mom"])
    df = pd.read_csv(path, skiprows=header_row)
    first_col = df.columns[0]
    df = df.rename(columns={first_col: "date"})
    df["date"] = pd.to_datetime(df["date"].astype(str), format="%Y%m%d", errors="coerce")
    df = df[df["date"].notna()].copy()

    mom_col = [c for c in df.columns if c.strip().lower() == "mom"]
    if len(mom_col) != 1:
        raise ValueError("Momentum column not found uniquely.")
    mom_col = mom_col[0]

    df[mom_col] = pd.to_numeric(df[mom_col], errors="coerce")
    df = df.replace([-99.99, -999.0, -999, -99.0], np.nan)
    df[mom_col] = df[mom_col] / 100.0
    df = df.rename(columns={mom_col: "Mom"})
    df = df.set_index("date").sort_index()
    return df[["Mom"]]

def ff_daily_to_periodic(ff_daily, runtime, target_index):
    """
    FF日次因子を ret_p と同じ periodic return に変換
    ret_p が週次/ 月次の単純収益なので、ここでも複利で変換する。
    """
    rule = runtime["rule"]  # 'ME' or 'W-FRI' etc.
    ff = ff_daily.copy()

    risk_cols = [c for c in ff.columns if c != "RF"]
    all_cols = ff.columns.tolist()

    ff_periodic = pd.DataFrame(index=ff.resample(rule).last().index, columns=all_cols, dtype=float)

    # RF 以外は複利
    for c in risk_cols:
        ff_periodic[c] = (1.0 + ff[c]).resample(rule).prod() - 1.0

    # RF も同様に複利で期間化
    ff_periodic["RF"] = (1.0 + ff["RF"]).resample(rule).prod() - 1.0

    ff_periodic = ff_periodic.reindex(target_index)
    return ff_periodic

ff5_path = "/mnt/data/F-F_Research_Data_5_Factors_2x3_daily.csv"
mom_path = "/mnt/data/F-F_Momentum_Factor_daily.csv"

ff5_d = load_ff5_daily_csv(ff5_path)
mom_d = load_ff_mom_daily_csv(mom_path)

ff_daily = ff5_d.join(mom_d, how="inner").sort_index()
ff_p = ff_daily_to_periodic(ff_daily, RUNTIME, ret_p.index)

display(ff_p.head())
display(ff_p.tail())
print(ff_p.columns.tolist())
```

このノートの `ret_p` は既に periodic return なので、それに `RF` を合わせて引きます。

```
# ret_p を FF の RF で超過収益化
common_idx = ret_p.index.intersection(ff_p.index)

ret_p_ff = ret_p.reindex(common_idx).copy()
ff_p = ff_p.reindex(common_idx).copy()

ret_p_excess = ret_p_ff.sub(ff_p["RF"], axis=0)

print("ret_p_excess shape:", ret_p_excess.shape)
display(ret_p_excess.head())
```

追加セル 3: 改良案1用の continuous TSFM を既存ノート変数で作成
==========================================

既存ノートは `compute_factor_mom`, `allocate_factor_weights` を既に持っていますが、  
改良案1では**連続スケーリング**にしたいので別名で作ります。

```
def rolling_factor_vol(factor_ret, window_periods=12, min_periods=6):
    return factor_ret.rolling(window_periods, min_periods=min_periods).std()

def normalize_long_only_series(w):
    w = w.clip(lower=0.0)
    s = w.sum()
    if s > 0:
        return w / s
    return w * 0.0

def normalize_ls_series(w):
    s = w.abs().sum()
    if s > 0:
        return w / s
    return w * 0.0

# 既存ノートの lookback 設定をそのまま流用
factor_mom_cont = factor_mom.copy()

signal_vol = rolling_factor_vol(
    factor_ret,
    window_periods=max(4, int(round(RUNTIME["periods_per_year"] / 4))),
    min_periods=max(3, int(round(RUNTIME["periods_per_year"] / 8)))
)

signal_scaled = factor_mom_cont / signal_vol.replace(0, np.nan)
signal_scaled = signal_scaled.clip(-3.0, 3.0)

weights_factor_cont = pd.DataFrame(index=signal_scaled.index, columns=signal_scaled.columns, dtype=float)

for t in signal_scaled.index:
    x = signal_scaled.loc[t].dropna()
    if len(x) == 0:
        weights_factor_cont.loc[t] = 0.0
        continue

    if CONFIG.get("long_only", True):
        weights_factor_cont.loc[t] = normalize_long_only_series(signal_scaled.loc[t].fillna(0.0))
    else:
        weights_factor_cont.loc[t] = normalize_ls_series(signal_scaled.loc[t].fillna(0.0))

weights_factor_cont = weights_factor_cont.fillna(0.0)

display(weights_factor_cont.tail())
```

```
# 既存ノートの factor target return

    weights_factor_cont.shift(1).reindex(factor_ret.index).fillna(0.0) * factor_ret
).sum(axis=1).rename("timed_factor_cont")

raw_factor_ret = factor_ret.mean(axis=1).rename("raw_factor_eq")

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 4))
((1 + pd.concat([raw_factor_ret, timed_factor_ret_cont], axis=1).dropna()).cumprod()).plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.8)

plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()
```

追加セル 5: 既存 `map_loadings_to_etf` を使って continuous TSFM を ETF に写像

```
weights_s2l_cont_dict = {}
skipped_s2l_cont = 0

for t in factor_mom_cont.index:
    if t not in loadings_by_t:
        skipped_s2l_cont += 1
        continue
    if t not in eligibility_mask_by_t:
        skipped_s2l_cont += 1
        continue

    L_t = loadings_by_t[t]
    elig_t = eligibility_mask_by_t[t]
    w_factor_t = weights_factor_cont.loc[t]

    w_etf_t = map_loadings_to_etf(
        loadings_t=L_t,
        w_factor=w_factor_t,

    equity_map={"S2-L continuous": equity_s2l_cont},

    title_prefix=f"S2-L Continuous TSFM | {RUNTIME['frequency_label']}"
)
```

追加セル 6: 改良案2の conditional-beta mapping（既存ノート名に合わせた版）
====================================================

既存ノートでは `estimate_regression_betas` があり、これは時点 `t` の rolling regression beta を返します。  
改良案2では、そこに ETF 特性を入れて beta を cross-section で予測します。

```
# ETF characteristic 作成（ret_p ベース）
char_mom12 = ret_p.shift(2).rolling(max(2, int(round(RUNTIME["periods_per_year"] * 12 / 12)))).sum()
char_rev1 = -ret_p.shift(1)
char_vol12 = ret_p.rolling(max(4, int(round(RUNTIME["periods_per_year"] / 4)))).std()

char_dict = {
    "mom12": char_mom12,
    "rev1": char_rev1,
    "vol12": char_vol12,
}

def zscore_cross_section(df):
    z = df.copy()
    for t in z.index:
        row = z.loc[t]
        mu = row.mean()
        sd = row.std(ddof=1)
        if pd.isna(sd) or sd == 0:
            z.loc[t] = np.nan
        else:
            z.loc[t] = (row - mu) / sd
    return z

chars_std = {k: zscore_cross_section(v) for k, v in char_dict.items()}
```

```
def predict_conditional_betas_existing_notebook(ret_p, factor_ret, chars_std, runtime):
    """
    既存 estimate_regression_betas を利用して beta を出し、
    その beta を ETF 特性で cross-section 回帰して beta_hat を作る。
    """
    pred_betas = {}
    factor_cols = list(factor_ret.columns)

    for t in ret_p.index:
        beta_df, elig_reg_t = estimate_regression_betas(
            ret_p=ret_p,
            factor_ret=factor_ret,
            t=t,
            window_periods=runtime["reg_window"],
            min_obs=runtime["min_obs"]
        )

        if beta_df is None or len(beta_df) == 0:
            continue

        z_parts = []
        for name, zdf in chars_std.items():
            if t in zdf.index:
                z_parts.append(zdf.loc[t].rename(name))
        if len(z_parts) == 0:
            continue

        Z = pd.concat(z_parts, axis=1)
        Z = Z.reindex(beta_df.index)

        beta_hat_df = pd.DataFrame(index=beta_df.index, columns=factor_cols, dtype=float)

        for fac in factor_cols:
            y = beta_df[fac]
            df = pd.concat([y.rename("y"), Z], axis=1).dropna()
            if len(df) < max(5, Z.shape[1] + 2):
                continue
            Y = df["y"]
            X = sm.add_constant(df.drop(columns="y"))
            res = sm.OLS(Y, X).fit()

            X_all = sm.add_constant(Z, has_constant="add")
            X_all = X_all.reindex(columns=X.columns, fill_value=0.0)
            beta_hat_df.loc[X_all.index, fac] = res.predict(X_all)

        pred_betas[t] = beta_hat_df

    return pred_betas

pred_cond_betas = predict_conditional_betas_existing_notebook(
    ret_p=ret_p,
    factor_ret=factor_ret,
    chars_std=chars_std,
    runtime=RUNTIME
)

print("pred_cond_betas dates:", len(pred_cond_betas))
sample_t = sorted(pred_cond_betas.keys())[-1]
display(pred_cond_betas[sample_t].head())
```

```
def map_conditional_betas_to_etf(beta_hat_t, w_factor, elig_mask_t, cap=None):
    all_assets = elig_mask_t.index

    fac = beta_hat_t.columns.intersection(w_factor.index)
    if len(fac) == 0:
        return pd.Series(0.0, index=all_assets)

    raw = beta_hat_t[fac].dot(w_factor[fac])
    w = pd.Series(0.0, index=all_assets)

    raw = raw.reindex(all_assets).fillna(0.0)
    raw[~elig_mask_t.reindex(all_assets).fillna(False)] = 0.0

    if CONFIG.get("long_only", True):
        w = normalize_long_only_series(raw)
    else:
        w = normalize_ls_series(raw)

    w = apply_weight_cap(w, cap=cap)
    return w

weights_s2cb_dict = {}
skipped_s2cb = 0

for t in factor_mom_cont.index:
    if t not in pred_cond_betas:
        skipped_s2cb += 1
        continue
    if t not in eligibility_mask_by_t:
        skipped_s2cb += 1
        continue

    beta_hat_t = pred_cond_betas[t]
    elig_t = eligibility_mask_by_t[t]
    w_factor_t = weights_factor_cont.loc[t]

    w_etf_t = map_conditional_betas_to_etf(
        beta_hat_t=beta_hat_t,
        w_factor=w_factor_t,
        elig_mask_t=elig_t,
        cap=CONFIG.get("etf_weight_cap", None)
    )
    weights_s2cb_dict[t] = w_etf_t

weights_s2cb = pd.DataFrame(weights_s2cb_dict).T.sort_index().fillna(0.0)

gross_s2cb, net_s2cb, turnover_s2cb, equity_s2cb, dd_s2cb = run_backtest(
    weights_s2cb,
    ret_p,
    CONFIG["cost_bps"]
)

print(f"S2-CB decision periods: {len(weights_s2cb)} (skipped={skipped_s2cb})")

plot_equity_dd(
    equity_map={"S2-CB": equity_s2cb},
    dd_map={"S2-CB": dd_s2cb},
    title_prefix=f"S2-CB (Conditional Beta Mapping) | {RUNTIME['frequency_label']}"
)
```

* * *

追加セル 7: 改良案3の Fama-French residualization を `ret_p` / `RUNTIME` ベースで実装
======================================================================

ここは既存ノートに完全に寄せた重要セルです。  
`ret_p_excess` に対して rolling residualization を行い、その residual series に対して再度 `build_rolling_pca` をかけます。

```
factor_cols_ff = ["Mkt-RF", "SMB", "HML", "RMW", "CMA", "Mom"]

def residualize_ret_p_against_ff(ret_p_excess, ff_p, runtime, factor_cols):
    resid = pd.DataFrame(index=ret_p_excess.index, columns=ret_p_excess.columns, dtype=float)
    beta_store = {}

    window_periods = runtime["reg_window"]
    min_obs = runtime["min_obs"]

    idx = ret_p_excess.index.intersection(ff_p.index)

    for i, t in enumerate(idx):
        start = max(0, i - window_periods + 1)
        win_idx = idx[start:i+1]

        X_win = ff_p.loc[win_idx, factor_cols]
        X_now = ff_p.loc[[t], factor_cols]

        beta_df = pd.DataFrame(index=ret_p_excess.columns, columns=factor_cols, dtype=float)

        for etf in ret_p_excess.columns:
            y_win = ret_p_excess.loc[win_idx, etf]
            df = pd.concat([y_win.rename("y"), X_win], axis=1).dropna()
            if len(df) < min_obs:
                continue

            Y = df["y"]
            X = sm.add_constant(df[factor_cols])
            res = sm.OLS(Y, X).fit()

            x_now = sm.add_constant(X_now, has_constant="add")
            x_now = x_now.reindex(columns=X.columns, fill_value=0.0)

            y_hat = float(res.predict(x_now).iloc[0])
            if pd.notna(ret_p_excess.loc[t, etf]):
                resid.loc[t, etf] = ret_p_excess.loc[t, etf] - y_hat

            beta_df.loc[etf] = res.params.reindex(["const"] + factor_cols).drop("const").values

        beta_store[t] = beta_df

    return resid, beta_store

ret_p_resid_ff, rolling_ff_betas = residualize_ret_p_against_ff(
    ret_p_excess=ret_p_excess,
    ff_p=ff_p,
    runtime=RUNTIME,
    factor_cols=factor_cols_ff
)

display(ret_p_resid_ff.head())
display(ret_p_resid_ff.tail())
```

追加セル 11: 伝統因子 attribution 表（既存ノートの戦略シリーズ名に合わせる）
===============================================

```
def ff_attr_table(strategy_dict, ff_p, factor_cols, nw_lags=3):
    rows = []
    for name, r in strategy_dict.items():
        if r is None or len(pd.Series(r).dropna()) == 0:
            continue
        res = ols_with_hac(r, ff_p[factor_cols], nw_lags=nw_lags)
        row = {"strategy": name, "alpha": res.params["const"], "alpha_t": res.tvalues["const"], "R2": res.rsquared}
        for c in factor_cols:
            row[c] = res.params.get(c, np.nan)
            row[f"{c}_t"] = res.tvalues.get(c, np.nan)
        rows.append(row)
    return pd.DataFrame(rows).set_index("strategy")

table_ff_attr = ff_attr_table(
    strategy_dict={
        "S2-L base": net_s2l if "net_s2l" in globals() else None,
        "S2-R base": net_s2r if "net_s2r" in globals() else None,
        "S2-L continuous": net_s2l_cont if "net_s2l_cont" in globals() else None,
        "S2-CB": net_s2cb if "net_s2cb" in globals() else None,
        "S2-L residual FF": net_s2l_resid_ff if "net_s2l_resid_ff" in globals() else None,
        "EQW": eqw_net if "eqw_net" in globals() else None,
    },
    ff_p=ff_p,
    factor_cols=factor_cols_ff,
    nw_lags=3
)

display(table_ff_attr)
```

追加セル 13: explained / unexplained decomposition

```
res_decomp = ols_with_hac(target_strategy, ff_p[factor_cols_ff], nw_lags=3)

df_decomp = pd.concat([
    pd.Series(target_strategy).rename("strategy"),
    ff_p[factor_cols_ff]
], axis=1).dropna()

X_full = sm.add_constant(df_decomp[factor_cols_ff], has_constant="add")
df_decomp["explained"] = res_decomp.predict(X_full)
df_decomp["unexplained"] = df_decomp["strategy"] - df_decomp["explained"]

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 6))
((1 + df_decomp[["strategy", "explained", "unexplained"]]).cumprod()).plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.8)
```

追加セル 14: PCA 因子の FF 帰属
======================

```
rows = []
for c in factor_ret.columns:
    res = ols_with_hac(factor_ret[c], ff_p[factor_cols_ff], nw_lags=3)
    row = {"factor": c, "alpha": res.params["const"], "alpha_t": res.tvalues["const"], "R2": res.rsquared}
    for f in factor_cols_ff:
        row[f] = res.params.get(f, np.nan)
        row[f"{f}_t"] = res.tvalues.get(f, np.nan)
    rows.append(row)

table_pca_ff_attr = pd.DataFrame(rows).set_index("factor")
display(table_pca_ff_attr)

heatmap_df = table_pca_ff_attr[factor_cols_ff].copy()

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(8, 4))
im = ax.imshow(heatmap_df.values, aspect="auto")
ax.set_xticks(range(len(heatmap_df.columns)))
ax.set_xticklabels(heatmap_df.columns, rotation=45, ha="right")
ax.set_yticks(range(len(heatmap_df.index)))
ax.set_yticklabels(heatmap_df.index)
ax.set_title("PCA Factors Regressed on FF5 + Mom")
fig.colorbar(im, ax=ax, fraction=0.046, pad=0.04)
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()
```

* * *

追加セル 15: 最終比較表
==============

```
metrics = pd.concat([
    calc_metrics(net_s2l, turnover_s2l, RUNTIME["periods_per_year"]).rename("S2-L base") if "net_s2l" in globals() else None,
    calc_metrics(net_s2r, turnover_s2r, RUNTIME["periods_per_year"]).rename("S2-R base") if "net_s2r" in globals() else None,
    calc_metrics(net_s2l_cont, turnover_s2l_cont, RUNTIME["periods_per_year"]).rename("S2-L continuous") if "net_s2l_cont" in globals() else None,
    calc_metrics(net_s2cb, turnover_s2cb, RUNTIME["periods_per_year"]).rename("S2-CB") if "net_s2cb" in globals() else None,
    calc_metrics(net_s2l_resid_ff, turnover_s2l_resid_ff, RUNTIME["periods_per_year"]).rename("S2-L residual FF") if "net_s2l_resid_ff" in globals() else None,
    calc_metrics(eqw_net, eqw_turnover, RUNTIME["periods_per_year"]).rename("EQW") if "eqw_net" in globals() else None,
], axis=1).T

display(metrics)

compare_plot = pd.concat([
    equity_s2l.rename("S2-L base") if "equity_s2l" in globals() else None,
    equity_s2l_cont.rename("S2-L continuous") if "equity_s2l_cont" in globals() else None,
    equity_s2cb.rename("S2-CB") if "equity_s2cb" in globals() else None,
    equity_s2l_resid_ff.rename("S2-L residual FF") if "equity_s2l_resid_ff" in globals() else None,
    eqw_equity.rename("EQW") if "eqw_equity" in globals() else None,
], axis=1).dropna(how="all")

fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(12, 6))
compare_plot.plot(ax=ax, linewidth=1.8)
ax.set_title(f"All Strategy Paths | {RUNTIME['frequency_label']}")
ax.set_ylabel("Equity")
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()
```

* * *

どこが「既存ノート対応」か
-------------

この版は、前の汎用コードと違って、次を完全に合わせています。

*   `ret_p` を主系列として使う
*   `RUNTIME["rule"]`, `RUNTIME["periods_per_year"]`, `RUNTIME["reg_window"]`, `RUNTIME["min_obs"]` を使う
*   `build_rolling_pca` を再利用する
*   `map_loadings_to_etf` を再利用する
*   `estimate_regression_betas` を改良案2で再利用する
*   `run_backtest`, `calc_metrics`, `plot_equity_dd` をそのまま使う
*   因子列は `F1, F2, ...`
*   loadings は既存ノート通り **DataFrame** 前提

* * *

最後に
---

このまま入れれば、あなたのノートは

*   既存の S2-L / S2-R
*   continuous TSFM
*   conditional-beta mapping
*   FF residualized theme strategy
*   FF attribution / decomposition

まで、**既存の構造を壊さずに拡張**できます。

次に必要なら、  
**この追加セル群を「既存ノートの Cell 28 の後、Cell 37 の後…」のように、セル番号ベースで差し込み位置まで指定**します。
